class="prc-TooltipV2-Tooltip-cYMVY" data-direction="nw" aria-hidden="true" id=":R3tv6fal9lab:">Edit and raw actions</span></div></div></div></div><div></div></div><div class="Box-sc-g0xbh4-0 hGyMdv"><section aria-labelledby="file-name-id-wide file-name-id-mobile" class="Box-sc-g0xbh4-0 fGqKFv"><div class="Box-sc-g0xbh4-0 eoaCFS js-snippet-clipboard-copy-unpositioned undefined" data-hpc="true"><article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Thirdwing Drupal 6 to Drupal 11 Migration</h1><a id="user-content-thirdwing-drupal-6-to-drupal-11-migration" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Thirdwing Drupal 6 to Drupal 11 Migration" href="#thirdwing-drupal-6-to-drupal-11-migration"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">A comprehensive migration system for the Thirdwing music organization, designed to migrate from Drupal 6 to Drupal 11 with ongoing incremental content synchronization.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🎯 Project Overview</h2><a id="user-content--project-overview" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🎯 Project Overview" href="#-project-overview"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This migration project enables seamless content migration from a legacy D6 site to a modern D11 platform while maintaining ongoing synchronization during the transition period. The system supports both complete initial migration and incremental content updates.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Migration Strategy</h3><a id="user-content-migration-strategy" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Migration Strategy" href="#migration-strategy"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Initially the module will be installed on a clean drupal installation.
Old site will remain active until new site is complete and acts as backup for all data.
Regular syncs from old to new with updated content.</p>
<p dir="auto">The architecture supports:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Clean D11 Installation</strong>: Designed for fresh installations only</li>
<li><strong>Complete Incremental Migration</strong>: Ongoing content synchronization between sites with automated conflict resolution</li>
<li><strong>Modern Media Architecture</strong>: Complete node-to-media conversion framework</li>
<li><strong>Comprehensive Content Migration</strong>: All content types and relationships preserved</li>
<li><strong>Modern Drupal Patterns</strong>: Uses D11 core modules and best practices</li>
<li><strong>Production-Safe Operations</strong>: Dual-site operation during transition with comprehensive testing</li>
<li><strong>Automated Setup &amp; Validation</strong>: Complete setup automation with built-in validation system</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Content Profile Integration</h3><a id="user-content-content-profile-integration" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Content Profile Integration" href="#content-profile-integration"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The D6 site uses the <strong>Content Profile</strong> module where profile data is stored as <code>profiel</code> content type nodes linked to users. The migration system properly handles:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Content Profile Fields</strong>: All profile fields from <code>content_type_profiel</code> table</li>
<li><strong>User-Profile Relationships</strong>: Links between users and their profile nodes</li>
<li><strong>Field Mapping</strong>: Complete mapping of Dutch profile fields (voornaam, achternaam, geslacht, etc.)</li>
<li><strong>Function Fields</strong>: All committee and role function fields</li>
<li><strong>Administrative Fields</strong>: Notes, email monitoring, and other administrative data</li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🏗️ Architecture Overview</h2><a id="user-content-️-architecture-overview" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🏗️ Architecture Overview" href="#️-architecture-overview"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Source Content Types (Drupal 6)</h3><a id="user-content-source-content-types-drupal-6" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Source Content Types (Drupal 6)" href="#source-content-types-drupal-6"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Content Types Migrated to D11 Nodes</strong>:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>activiteit</code> (activities) → <code>activiteit</code></li>
<li><code>repertoire</code> (musical repertoire) → <code>repertoire</code></li>
<li><code>nieuws</code> (news articles) → <code>nieuws</code></li>
<li><code>pagina</code> (pages) → <code>pagina</code></li>
<li><code>foto</code> (photo albums) → <code>foto</code></li>
<li><code>locatie</code> (venues) → <code>locatie</code></li>
<li><code>vriend</code> (friends/partners) → <code>vriend</code></li>
<li><code>profiel</code> (user profiles) → User profile fields (Content Profile integration)</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Content Types Converted to Media Entities</strong>:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>verslag</code> (meeting reports) → <code>document</code> media</li>
<li><code>audio</code> (audio recordings) → <code>audio</code> media</li>
<li><code>video</code> (video recordings) → <code>video</code> media</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Content Types Excluded</strong>:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>nieuwsbrief</code> (newsletters) - Not migrated</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Content Profile System</h3><a id="user-content-content-profile-system" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Content Profile System" href="#content-profile-system"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The D6 site uses <strong>Content Profile</strong> module with profile data stored in:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong><code>content_type_profiel</code></strong> table (CCK/content type table)</li>
<li><strong>Profile nodes</strong> linked to users via the <code>uid</code> field</li>
<li><strong>Profile fields</strong> mapped to D11 user fields:</li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Bundle-Based Organization</h4><a id="user-content-bundle-based-organization" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Bundle-Based Organization" href="#bundle-based-organization"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Document Media</strong>: All documents, sheet music, reports</li>

</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Access Control System</h3><a id="user-content-access-control-system" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Access Control System" href="#access-control-system"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Permissions by Term Integration</strong>:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>field_access_terms</code> on all content types</li>
<li><code>field_media_access</code> on all media entities</li>
<li>Taxonomy-based permissions for both nodes and media</li>
<li>Role-based access control through taxonomy terms</li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Prerequisites</h3><a id="user-content-prerequisites" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Prerequisites" href="#prerequisites"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Drupal 11</strong>: Fresh installation</li>
<li><strong>PHP 8.2+</strong>: With required extensions</li>
<li><strong>Database</strong>: MySQL 8.0+ or PostgreSQL 13+</li>
<li><strong>Migration Database</strong>: Read-only access to D6 database</li>
</ul>

  'database' =&gt; 'drupal6_database',
  'username' =&gt; 'db_user', 
  'password' =&gt; 'db_password',
  'host' =&gt; 'localhost',
  'port' =&gt; '3306',
  'driver' =&gt; 'mysql',
  'prefix' =&gt; '',
];"><pre><span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-c1">$</span>databases</span>[<span class="pl-s">'<span class="pl-s">migrate</span>'</span>][<span class="pl-s">'<span class="pl-s">default</span>'</span>] = [

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">4. <div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Reset any stuck migrations
drush migrate:reset-status d6_thirdwing_user

# Test user migration
drush migrate:import d6_thirdwing_user --limit=5

# Initial full migration
./modules/custom/thirdwing_migrate/scripts/migrate-execute.sh

# Regular incremental sync
./modules/custom/thirdwing_migrate/scripts/migrate-sync.sh --since=&quot;last-week&quot;"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Reset any stuck migrations</span>
drush migrate:reset-status d6_thirdwing_user

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Test user migration</span>
drush migrate:import d6_thirdwing_user --limit=5

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Key Migration Features</h3><a id="user-content-key-migration-features" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Key Migration Features" href="#key-migration-features"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Incremental Migration Support</strong>: Delta migrations with timestamp-based filtering
<strong>Content Profile Integration</strong>: ✅ <strong>FIXED</strong> - Proper handling of Content Profile data from <code>content_type_profiel</code> table
<strong>Robust Error Handling</strong>: Comprehensive data validation and error recovery
<strong>Memory Management</strong>: Optimized for large datasets with batch processing<br>
<strong>Dependency Management</strong>: Proper migration sequencing and relationship handling
<strong>Data Integrity</strong>: Complete preservation of content relationships with old site as single source of truth
<strong>Conflict Resolution</strong>: Handle content modified on both old and new sites</p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Content Profile Migration ✅ <strong>RESOLVED</strong></h4><a id="user-content-content-profile-migration--resolved" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Content Profile Migration ✅ RESOLVED" href="#content-profile-migration--resolved"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Issue</strong>: Migration failed with <code>profile_values</code> table not found error</li>
<li><strong>Root Cause</strong>: D6 site uses Content Profile module, not traditional Profile module</li>
<li><strong>Solution</strong>: Updated source plugins to read from <code>content_type_profiel</code> table</li>
<li><strong>Result</strong>: User migration now works with complete profile field mapping</li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Phase 2: Core Migration Completion (Immediate)</h3><a id="user-content-phase-2-core-migration-completion-immediate" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Phase 2: Core Migration Completion (Immediate)" href="#phase-2-core-migration-completion-immediate"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol start="7" dir="auto">
<li><strong>Advanced Media Migration</strong> - Convert files to media entities with context-based categorization</li>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Incremental Migration Strategy</h3><a id="user-content-incremental-migration-strategy" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Incremental Migration Strategy" href="#incremental-migration-strategy"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Regular Content Sync Capabilities</h4><a id="user-content-regular-content-sync-capabilities" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Regular Content Sync Capabilities" href="#regular-content-sync-capabilities"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Delta Migration</strong>: Import only new and changed content since last sync</li>
<li><strong>Timestamp-Based Filtering</strong>: Track content changes using <code>created</code> and <code>changed</code> dates</li>
<li><strong>Conflict Resolution</strong>: Handle content modified on both old and new sites</li>
<li><strong>Safe Sync Operations</strong>: Preserve new site modifications while importing updates</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Incremental Migration Features</h4><a id="user-content-incremental-migration-features" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Incremental Migration Features" href="#incremental-migration-features"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Initial full migration
./migrate-execute.sh --mode=full

# Regular incremental sync (daily/weekly)
./migrate-sync.sh --since=&quot;2025-01-01&quot;

# Sync specific content types
./migrate-sync.sh --content-types=&quot;nieuws,activiteit&quot; --since=&quot;last-week&quot;

# Preview changes before sync
./migrate-sync.sh --dry-run --since=&quot;yesterday&quot;"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Initial full migration</span>
./migrate-execute.sh --mode=full

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Regular incremental sync (daily/weekly)</span>
./migrate-sync.sh --since=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>2025-01-01<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Sync specific content types</span>
./migrate-sync.sh --content-types=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>nieuws,activiteit<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> --since=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>last-week<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Preview changes before sync</span>
./migrate-sync.sh --dry-run --since=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>yesterday<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Change Detection &amp; Tracking</h4><a id="user-content-change-detection--tracking" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Change Detection &amp; Tracking" href="#change-detection--tracking"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Modified Content Detection</strong>: Track changes via <code>node.changed</code> timestamps</li>
<li><strong>New Content Identification</strong>: Identify content created since last sync</li>
<li><strong>Deleted Content Handling</strong>: Optional handling of content deleted from D6</li>
<li><strong>User Activity Tracking</strong>: Track new user registrations and profile updates</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Sync Safety Features</h4><a id="user-content-sync-safety-features" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Sync Safety Features" href="#sync-safety-features"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Backup Before Sync</strong>: Automatic database backup before incremental migration</li>
<li><strong>Rollback Capability</strong>: Ability to revert incremental changes if needed</li>
<li><strong>Simple Conflict Resolution</strong>: Always overwrite new site changes with old site content (old site is authoritative)</li>
<li><strong>Validation Checks</strong>: Verify data integrity after each sync operation</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">📄 License</h2><a id="user-content--license" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 📄 License" href="#-license"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This migration project is designed for the specific Thirdwing music organization but can serve as a reference implementation for similar D6 to D11 migrations with incremental sync requirements.</p>
<hr>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Note</strong>: This migration project supports both initial full migration and ongoing incremental content synchronization, enabling safe dual-site operation during the transition period. The old D6 site remains active and serves as the primary data source until the new D11 site is ready for production cutover.</p>
